***столь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>столь</a> (902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>столь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stolʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>so, such
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>Столь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>столь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:маленький.html>ма́ло</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stolʹ</b> mnógo, <b>stolʹ</b> málo.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">So much, so little.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>столь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stolʹ</b> že</i> ― <span class="e-translation">equally</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настолько.html>насто́лько</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nastólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***столько.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a> (18266)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>this much, this long</li>
<li>so much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:устать.html>уста́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голодный.html>го́лоден</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja ne <b>stólʹko</b> ustál, skólʹko góloden</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I’m not as tired as I am hungry.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stólʹko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>this/that much/many</li>
<li>so much, so many
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stólʹko</b> vrémeni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">so much time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столько.html>сто́лько</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stólʹko</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation">so many books</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стольник.html>сто́льник</a> (32069)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/столъRussian"><a href = vnd.unilang:столь.html>сто́ль</a></a> + <a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/-никRussian">-ник</a>  ( stol' - table + nik - masculine noun suffix <a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reforms_of_Russian_orthographyThe_post-revolution_reform">(Pre-1918 reform orthography ) </a> )

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столяр.html>столя́р</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stoljár</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stoljárnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>joiner's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мастерская.html>мастерска́я</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stoljárnaja</b> masterskája</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>joiner's</b> shop</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ремесло.html>ремесло́</a>; <b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stoljárnoje</b> remesló; <b>stoljárnoje</b> délo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">joinery; <b>joiner's</b> work</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:верстак.html>верста́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stoljárnyj</b> versták</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>joiner's</b> bench</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клей.html>клей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stoljárnyj</b> klej</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>joiner's</b> glue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:столярный.html>столя́рные</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:изделие.html>изде́лия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stoljárnyje</b> izdélija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">woodwork; finish</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***стонать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стонать.html>стона́ть</a> (4071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">стонати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stonati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stenàti</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:стон.html>стон</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ston</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">stonati</i>. Non-Slavic cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">στόνος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stónos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a sighing or groaning</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tonō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to thunder, to resound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्तनति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stanati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roar, to cry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стонать.html>стона́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stonátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застонать.html>застона́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простонать.html>простона́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to groan, to moan</li>
<li>to suffer, to languish</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:застонать.html>застона́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastonátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простонать.html>простона́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prostonátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стопа.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопа</a> (9085)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопа́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stopá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопы́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стоп</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> foot</li>
<li>footstep</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>Russian usually does not distinguish between "leg" and "foot," and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nogá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is used for both. Use <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопа</a></b> only when it is vital to make the distinction, as in medical situations.<i></i>
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нога.html>нога́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nogá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступня.html>ступня́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stupnjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">šag</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стопка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стопка.html>сто́пка</a> (6163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоп.html>стопа́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stopá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стопка.html>сто́пка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stópka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стопка.html>сто́пки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стопка.html>сто́пки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стопка.html>сто́пок</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стопа́рик</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стопочка.html>сто́почка</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pile, rouleau</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:топтать.html>топта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">toptátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторицей.html>стори́цей</a> (30083)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторицей.html>стори́цей</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">storícej</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(antiquated)</i> hundredfold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>земля́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:родить.html>роди́т</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторицей.html>стори́цей</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Zemljá rodít <b>storícej</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">The soil will produce a hundredfold (said of a good harvest).</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сторож.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторожа.html>сторож</a> (7205)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сторожь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">storožĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*storžь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">guard</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*storʔg-</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стража.html>страж</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">straž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожа.html>сто́рож</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stórož</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожа.html>сто́рожа</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожа.html>сторожа́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожа.html>стороже́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>watch, watchman, guard, custodian</li></ol>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторожевой.html>сторожево́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дно</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>storoževóje</b> súdno</i> ― <span class="e-translation">patrol ship</span></div></dd>

***сторона.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторона́</a> (121)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*storna</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sterh₃-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">structure</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">strategy</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:страна.html>страна́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">straná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from old Church Slavonic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторона́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">storoná</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́роны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторо́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>side, hand, party
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:левый.html>ле́вой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s lévoj <b>storoný</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the left side</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s odnój storoný</i> ― <span class="e-translation">on the one hand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>той</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:улица.html>у́лицы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na toj <b>storoné</b> úlicy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">across the street</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зритель.html>зри́телей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>stóronu</b> ot zrítelej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">aside from the audience</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>direction, quarter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:какой.html>како́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ветер.html>ве́тер</a>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s kakój <b>storoný</b> véter?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">from what direction is the wind blowing?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороны́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">četýre storoný svéta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the four cardinal points</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>place, region, country
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ná storonu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">abroad</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>distance
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>стороне́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>storoné</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">aloof, aside</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сто́рону</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>stóronu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">aside, apart</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сторониться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сторониться.html>сторони́ться</a> (14577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторона.html>сторона́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">storoná</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сторониться.html>сторони́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">storonítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посторониться.html>посторони́ться</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to avoid, to shun, to eschew</li>

***стоянка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нка</a> (4456)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stojánka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stop, stand, station</li>
<li>(fixed) quarters</li>
<li>parking, parking lot (for cars)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоянка.html>стоя́нка</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запрещённый.html>запрещена́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Stojánka</b> zapreščená</i> ― <span class="e-translation">No parking</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>anchorage</li></ol>

***стоять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a> (99)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стоꙗти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stojati</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stand</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*stoh₂-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stojátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:постоять.html>постоя́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to stand, to be situated</li>
<li>to stop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with most of the conjugation forms pertaining to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоить.html>сто́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stóitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выста́иваться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vystáivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">доста́ивать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">dostáivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заста́иваться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zastáivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>стоя́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stojátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jáčij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stojáčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>standing, stand-up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčeje</b> položénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standing posture</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:положение.html>положе́нии</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>челове́ке</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тном</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>stojáčem</b> položénii (o čelovéke, živótnom)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standing</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лампа.html>ла́мпа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčaja</b> lámpa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">table/desk lamp</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воротник.html>воротни́к</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:воротничок.html>воротничо́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčij</b> vorotník/vorotničók</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stand-up collar</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčije</b> mesta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standing room</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бусе</a> 50 <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чих</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>мест</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v avtóbuse 50 <b>stojáčix</b> mest</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the bus has standing room for 50 persons</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>stagnant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вода.html>вода́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčaja</b> vodá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">stagnant water</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стоячий.html>стоя́чие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волны</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stojáčije</b> volny</i> ― <span class="e-translation">standing/stationary waves</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> erect, up, with a hard-on</li></ol>
